Bobbi Brown Hydrating Foundation>>Water,Glycerin,Mineral Oil,Polysorbate 20,Sodium Hyaluronate,Octocrylene,Tetrasodium EDTA,Phenoxyethanol,Ethylhexylglycerin,Fragrance,,Please note: The ingredients listed are from company websites and databases and may vary from product to product.,,Skin Types,,Skin types are a categorization of the skin according to its natural protective function,the color,and thickness. There are three skin types: normal,dry,and oily.,,Normal Skin,,Normal skin has a natural protective barrier with a good balance of water and lipids and the color is clear. Usually,the skin does not itch and does not show any visible signs of dryness or oiliness.,,Dry Skin,,Dry skin has a weakened or damaged protective barrier that lacks lipids and is more vulnerable to external aggressors. Dry skin can feel itchy and sometimes looks irritated.,,Oily Skin,,Oily skin has an excess of sebum that exceeds the skin’s natural protection,which causes a greasy look and feel. The skin can itch and sometimes look shiny.,,Skin Concerns,,If the skin concerns are known,they should be listed here.,,If there are no skin concerns,the field should be left blank.,,Skin Tone,,The tone of the skin can range from light to dark,depending on the amount of melanin in the skin.,,Light Skin Tone,,The skin tone ranges from fair to light.,,Medium Skin Tone,,The skin tone ranges from medium to dark.,,Dark Skin Tone,,The skin tone ranges from very dark to black.
